What started this, what created these Santa Ana winds here in Southern California? Let's show you what's going on in the atmosphere in terms of what we're dealing with here. We have this ridge of high pressure out in the Pacific, this area of low pressure out across the Great Basin. And that just dropped in just to the north of Southern California. And the pressure gradient in between these two systems helps to funnel in all of that wind energy down to the surface. And that wind energy is warming. It's compressing and it's drying things out. So this was the example I was using. If you're in between this tight pressure gradient here, that's you walking through two buildings on each side of you. And that wind really rushes in.
